But let me say that my boyfriend had already completed the process with the same paper I used. I don't want to say that it had anything to do with my appearance, but I'm sure it did. My boyfriend is of a lighter complexion than I am, and his phenotype does not predominantly look indigenous. Even though we are both Hispanic, he gets treated differently based on his skin tone. In the end, she said that she would allow it because they had allowed it for him. My experience was unpleasant, and if I had not stood up for myself, it would have been a waste of a trip to the DMV. If I had the wrong paper, the lady at the front assigning numbers and checking paperwork should have told me so then and there. Do better, DMV. Not all minorities will allow you to mistreat them.</Text>

< user_name>
Amy Fish<//user_name>
<review>I tried out floating for the first time today! I was nervous but there was no need for that! What a blissful experience.  The man at the front desk was friendly but not super helpful and I felt a little rushed with the instructions he gave me. He didn't give me the option to change my music or light color but I knew that was a possibility since I read the other reviews.  They have a sheet hanging up on the wall in the room with a few more tips so that was helpful. They advise showing up 15 minutes early but I would recommend 20 minutes so you don't feel rushed. Your float time starts right at your scheduled time so you have to shower and get ready before that. They offer free Classy Hippie Tea before and after your float which is so yummy and another reason to arrive a little earlier. Each room has a private shower and changing area next to the float tank. I was in room number 4 at the end of the hallway. You put your earplugs in (two different kinds to choose from) and then do a quick rinse and then hop in the tank (no swimsuit needed).

I used the Cosmic Om music (soft background music with bells and the om sounds) which was really nice and relaxing and the red-colored light. You can pick out your options at the front desk before your float. I didn't have time to listen to all the options. I wish they had them on their website so you could pick it ahead.  After about 5 minutes I turned off the light and halfway through I turned off the music. There are large buttons on the side of the tub to turn them on and off. With the music off I was able to hear my breath and relax my thoughts. With the lights off I felt like I was floating in space. I also picked an intention before I floated which was nice. I tried a few different positions with my arms such as at my sides, resting on my body or bent above my head. I found that I liked them above my head the most. They also have a small ring you can rest your head inside if you want. I felt completely relaxed afterward. It is an indescribable experience and I highly recommend you experience it yourself to see what it is like. I am looking forward to my next float!! Next time I want to try the infrared sauna or the Somadome (meditation pod) before my float.

Then you shower off all the salt. They provide shampoo and body wash and a washcloth. It is not organic though so bring your own if you want that. Afterward, make sure you allow yourself plenty of time in the post-float area to paint or draw, journal, read, drink tea, water or kombucha, stretch, or just relax. They have indoor and outdoor seating. They also have some CBD products and shirts/tanks to shop from.

The only problem I had was that I forgot to not shave my armpits so there was some burning. I put some Vaseline on which helped. Make sure not to shave any body parts before your float!

Also, they say you don't need to bring anything but if you are going out for a meal afterward I would suggest bringing a comb or brush, deodorant, etc. so you can get ready after your float. They have a small vanity area in the post-float area if you need a space to get ready. They provide everything else such as a towel and flip flops.

Afterward, if you want a healthy meal I suggest Vibe Health Bar (just next door) or Sun and Soil which is just about a 5-minute drive away. Both have organic and vegan cold-pressed juices and meals. Or the Strapping Store is just a couple of minutes' walk with really fun and unique gifts.< /review>< date>

<Rate>5< /Rate><Review>It is super easy to book a float or other services here.  I arrived and was greeted warmly and oriented to the experience.  The waiting area is delightful and has water, tea, and even kombucha (charge for non-members).  The float room has a place for personal items, a basket with items needed for before, during and after the float.  If you are mobility challenged as I am you can still do this... maybe not from a wheelchair, though. I have knee issues and was able to do it.  However, next time I will bring and wear some yoga socks which have a tread on the bottom so that I can feel more secure as the tub is very slippery.

The tub itself is roomy and when you close the door it is completely dark.  You have reachable light and sound options you can press... a blue light if you need it, and music is available.  I needed the light at one point to find the provided bottle of water.  Be careful getting in to not splash water up your nose... very uncomfortable.  Once settled, I had a wonderful float!

Here's the bonus: I booked this to follow a deep 90 minute massage and it integrated the massage most beautifully.</Review><pics>None< /pics><resp>None</resp>< gmapID>

<Review>As many others, I was introduced to floating through the Joe Rogan Experience podcast. It wasn't until Capitol Floats opened in 2016, when my wife got me a 3-float-pack for my birthday, that I had the opportunity to try it. I am grateful for her pushing me in this direction!

Looking back at when I started, I was going through some personal challenges that I knew I needed to find my way through and floating helped catapult me into a better, different state-of-mind. While its effects were immediate but temporary, it was exactly what I needed at that time. I quickly realized that this was something I needed to experiment with on a regular basis and so I did and now it is something I do regularly.

Since, floating has become an invaluable tool that has improved my overall well-being. The physical benefits alone are undeniable, creativity and introspection are significantly enhanced, and something about it just feels good. I often times come into each session with an intent to solve a problem or to brainstorm an idea and I find that the tank allows my mind to operate at a higher clip than normal. All-in-all, the ability to have these experiences reliably continues to help shape other experiences in my life in a meaningful way.

One of my favorite things about Capitol Floats are the humans! Every person I have met through Capitol Floats shares a special energy about them that makes you want to better yourself. I feel like these are folks that are consciously trying to live fulfilling lives while facing  their fears and challenges head on. It's very inspiring.

If I was going to give advice on floating, I would recommend you pee before you drop in and avoid getting salt in your eye (or don't forget your mini water bottle!)!!! Ha...in all seriousness, I would tell people to find what works for you! Floating has helped me, but it really starts by looking internally and trying to get a better understanding of why we all do whatever it is that we do. Floating is a tool to help you navigate through this life and it is up to you to use it and/or find the right tools that are going to help you be a better version of yourself.

Highly recommend people make this tool a part of their life!<//Review><rating>5< /rating>< GmapID>

<Review>Love this location. The tanks are built into the room not in a pod which makes it so much easier to relax.

After-float area is very comfortable and feels like you are in your living room. The tea is GREAT and if you're feeling creative they have sketch pads and any books to read.

I started floating as a way to relax my muscles and my mind. I have PTSD and found floating an amazing way to reset my mind. My first float I felt completely relaxed, every muscle in my body felt relief. It was euphoric and my anxiety was extremely low. You definitely have to book more than one session to fully benefit. You will learn after every float how to meditate and relax your mind until you fall asleep. If you can get to the point where you fall asleep you will feel amazing! Everyone is different so have an open mind when floating. It takes more than one float to know if it helps you. As a person with PTSD and anxiety it had been a miracle in my life.  Happy floating!<//Review><pictures>None</pictures>< Response>

<user_id>105974521297771826080</user_id>< user_name>
Hope ‚Äúdirtie hippie‚Äù Nuxoll<//user_name>
<Time>1512703291781< /Time><rate>5<//rate>< Text>
My float experience was a complete and utterly awesome mind body trip and a half.

They say each person experiences it differently so here is my version. First a little about me. I am a busy business owner who was in a car accident about a year ago that im still healing from. I am dealing with business thing from 7 am sometimes until midnight. Stress is no stranger to me. I also played roller derby for 8 yrs do my body needs some love.

I chose a complete sensory deprivation experience. I didnt expect that choice(because i have claustrophobic issues) but it came completely naturally. As soon as I entered the pod I wanted nothing to do with the world. I want to be one with the water. No lights, no sound, it was fabulous.

I discovered, of course, that I coud hear each sound the inside of my body made and that was reasuring and interesting. I played with that for a while much like a baby might in the womb. I turned around and round slowly(not onto my face, you cant get this salt water on your face).
I lost all sense of my relation to the space i was in. I didnt know which way the door was and I didnt care.

I bent my limbs and spine in odd but comfortable ways and trickled water and it echoed and sounded odd like i was on another planet. At some point i suppose i got tired of playing with movement and i just went still.

Mind you....this entire time.....

I DIDNT THINK OF WORK OR LIFE OUTSIDE THIS POD. I WAS MINDLESS. IT WAS FABULOUS!

in this new stillness in the pure blackness and pure silence....i became one with the water that was holding me up and the only way i want to describe it is to say i felt like i was being cradled by the most comfortable body temperature pudding ever. Hahaha it was thick and good and i didnt want to leave. That lasted maybe 10 or 15 minutes then they turned the lights on and i had to get out.

I rate this experience a 200+ and i want to do it once a month. I would go once a week but i cant afford that. I am very happy to have found this float experience and will keep going.< /Text>
